    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            SetCookie('SWScreenWidth', screen.width);
            SetCookie('SWClientWidth', document.body.clientWidth);
            
            $("div.ui-article:last").addClass("last-article");
            $("div.region .app:last").addClass("last-app");

            // get on screen alerts
            var isAnyActiveOSA = 'False';
            var onscreenAlertCookie = GetCookie('Alerts');

            if (onscreenAlertCookie == '' || onscreenAlertCookie == undefined) {
                onscreenAlertCookie = "";
            }
            if (isAnyActiveOSA == 'True') {
                GetContent(homeURL + "/cms/Tools/OnScreenAlerts/UserControls/OnScreenAlertDialogListWrapper.aspx?OnScreenAlertCookie=" + onscreenAlertCookie + "&SiteID=4", "onscreenalert-holder", 2, "OnScreenAlertCheckListItem();");
            }

            

        });

    // ADA SKIP NAV
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(document).on('focus', '#skipLink', function () {
            $("div.sw-skipnav-outerbar").animate({
                marginTop: "0px"
            }, 500);
        });

        $(document).on('blur', '#skipLink', function () {
            $("div.sw-skipnav-outerbar").animate({
                marginTop: "-30px"
            }, 500);
        });
    });

    // ADA MYSTART
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var top_level_nav = $('.sw-mystart-nav');

        // Set tabIndex to -1 so that top_level_links can't receive focus until menu is open
        // school dropdown
        $(top_level_nav).find('ul').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);

        // my account dropdown
        $(top_level_nav).next('ul').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);

        var openNavCallback = function(e, element) {
             // hide open menus
            hideMyStartBarMenu();

            // show school dropdown
            if ($(element).find('ul').length > 0) {
                $(element).find('.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $(element).find('.sw-dropdown').find('li:first-child a').focus()
            }

            // show my account dropdown
            if ($(element).next('ul').length > 0) {
                $(element).next('.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $(element).next('.sw-dropdown').find('li:first-child a').focus();
                $('#sw-mystart-account').addClass("clicked-state");
            }
        }

        $(top_level_nav).click(function (e) {
            openNavCallback(e, this);
        });

        $('.sw-dropdown-list li').click(function(e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();
            $(this).focus();
        });
        
        // Bind arrow keys for navigation
        $(top_level_nav).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 37) { //key left
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).prev('.sw-mystart-nav').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('div').find('.sw-mystart-nav').last().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                e.preventDefault();

                // show school dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('div.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }

                // show my account dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('ul.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 39) { //key right
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the last item
                if ($(this).next('.sw-mystart-nav').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('div').find('.sw-mystart-nav').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).next('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                e.preventDefault();

                // show school dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('div.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
                }

                // show my account dropdown
                if ($(this).next('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).next('ul.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 13 || e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                // If submenu is hidden, open it
                e.preventDefault();

                
                openNavCallback(e, this);
                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=true]').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27) { //escape key
                e.preventDefault();
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            } else {
                $(this).parent('.sw-mystart-nav').find('ul[aria-hidden=false] a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        // school dropdown
        var startbarlinks = $(top_level_nav).find('ul').find('a');
        bindMyStartBarLinks(startbarlinks);

        // my account dropdown
        var myaccountlinks = $(top_level_nav).next('ul').find('a');
        bindMyStartBarLinks(myaccountlinks);

        function bindMyStartBarLinks(links) {
            $(links).keydown(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();

                if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                    e.preventDefault();

                    // This is the first item
                    if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                        if ($(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').length > 0) {
                            $(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        } else {
                            $(this).parents('ul').prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                    }
                } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                    e.preventDefault();

                    if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                        if ($(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').length > 0) {
                            $(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        } else {
                            $(this).parents('ul').prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().attr('tabIndex', 0);
                        $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                    }
                } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) { // escape key or key left
                    e.preventDefault();
                    hideMyStartBarMenu();
                } else if (e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                    e.preventDefault();
                    window.location = $(this).attr('href');
                } else {
                    var found = false;

                    $(this).parent('div').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                        if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                            $(this).focus();
                            found = true;
                            return false;
                        }
                    });

                    if (!found) {
                        $(this).parent('div').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                            if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                                $(this).focus();
                                return false;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation
        $('#sw-mystart-inner').find('.sw-mystart-nav').last().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            }
        });

        /*$(document).click(function() { 
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });*/

        // try to capture as many custom MyStart bars as possible
        $('.sw-mystart-button').find('a').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-inner').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });

        $('ul.sw-dropdown-list').blur(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-mypasskey').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-sitemanager').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-myview').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-signin').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-register').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        // button click events
        $('div.sw-mystart-button.home a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.pw a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.manage a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-account').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).addClass('clicked-state');
                $('#sw-myaccount-list').show();
            }
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-mypasskey a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.signin a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.register a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });
    });

    function hideMyStartBarMenu() {
        $('.sw-dropdown').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').css('display', 'none');
        $('#sw-mystart-account').removeClass("clicked-state");
    }

    // ADA CHANNEL NAV
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var channelCount;
        var channelIndex = 1;
        var settings = {
            menuHoverClass: 'hover'
        };

        // Add ARIA roles to menubar and menu items
        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').attr('role', 'menubar').find('li a').attr('role', 'menuitem').attr('tabindex', '0');

        var top_level_links = $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('> li > a');
        channelCount = $(top_level_links).length;


        $(top_level_links).each(function() {
            $(this).attr('aria-posinset', channelIndex).attr('aria-setsize', channelCount);
            $(this).next('ul').attr({ 'aria-hidden': 'true', 'role': 'menu' });

            if ($(this).parent('li.sw-channel-item').children('ul').length > 0) {
                $(this).attr('aria-haspopup', 'true');
            }

            var sectionCount = $(this).next('ul').find('a').length;
            var sectionIndex = 1;
            $(this).next('ul').find('a').each(function() {
                $(this).attr('tabIndex', -1).attr('aria-posinset', sectionIndex).attr('aria-setsize', sectionCount);
                sectionIndex++;
            });
            channelIndex++;

        });

        $(top_level_links).focus(function () {
            //hide open menus
            hideChannelMenu();

            if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').css('display', 'block');
            }
        });

        // Bind arrow keys for navigation
        $(top_level_links).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 37) { //key left
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').last().find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 39) { //key right
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the last item
                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').first().find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).parent('li')
                         .addClass(settings.menuHoverClass)
                         .find('ul').css('display', 'block')
                         .attr('aria-hidden', 'false')
                         .find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0)
                         .first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 13 || e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                // If submenu is hidden, open it
                e.preventDefault();

                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=true]').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27) { //escape key
                e.preventDefault();
                hideChannelMenu();
            } else {
                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=false] a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        var links = $(top_level_links).parent('li').find('ul').find('a');

        $(links).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 38) {
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) {
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $(this).parents('ul').first().prev('a').focus().parents('ul').first().find('.' + settings.menuHoverClass).removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass);
            } else if (e.keyCode == 32) {
                e.preventDefault();
                window.location = $(this).attr('href');
            } else {
                var found = false;

                $(this).parent('li').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        found = true;
                        return false;
                    }
                });

                if (!found) {
                    $(this).parent('li').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                        if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                            $(this).focus();
                            return false;
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        function hideChannelMenu() {
            $('li.sw-channel-item.' + settings.menuHoverClass).removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').css('display', 'none').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);
        }
        
        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation
        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('a').last().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus
                hideChannelMenu();
            }
        });

        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('a').first().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // hide open MyStart Bar menus
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            }
        });

        /*$(document).click(function() {
            hideChannelMenu();
        });*/

        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });
    });

    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('input.required').each(function() {
            if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').length > 0) {
                if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').html().indexOf('recStar') < 0) {
                    $('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').prepend('<span class="recStar" aria-label="required item">*</span> ');
                }
            }
        });

        $(document).ajaxComplete(function() {
            $('input.required').each(function() {
                if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').length > 0) {
                    if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').html().indexOf('recStar') < 0) {
                        $('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').prepend('<span class="recStar" aria-label="required item">*</span> ');
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
    </script>

    <style type="text/css">/* MedaiBegin Standard *//*

@font-face {

<script type="text/javascript">
	var csKeyCodes = { "tab": 9, "enter": 13, "esc": 27, "space": 32, "end": 35, "home": 36, "left": 37, "up": 38, "right": 39, "down": 40, "shift": 16 };
	var windowHeight = $(window).height();
    
	$(window).load(function() {
		calendarListView();
		searchText();
        
        //ACCESSIBLE NAV APP
        $(".ui-widget.app.navigation").csAccessibleNavigationApp();
		
		//HIDE EMPTY DROPDOWN THAT GETS PLACED BY THE SYSTEM IF CHANNEL HAS NO SECTIONS BUT CHANNEL HOMEPAGE IS TURNED ON
		$("ul.sw-channel-dropdown").each(function() {
			var systemDropdown = $(this);
            $(this).wrap("<div class='sw-channel-dropdown-outer'></div>");
			if(!$("li",systemDropdown).length) {
				$(systemDropdown).remove();
			}
		});
        
        //DOC ADD HAS-DROPDOWN CLASS TO CHANNELS THAT HAVE A SECTION DROPDOWN
        $("li.sw-channel-item").each(function() {
			if($(".sw-channel-dropdown", this).length) {
				$(this).addClass("has-dropdown");
			}
		});
        
        $("#gb-channel-list-outer").show();
        
        var windowHeight = $(window).height();
        $(".hp #gb-template-top").height(windowHeight);
        $(".sp #gb-template-top").height($("#gb-channel-list-outer").height() + 118);
        if($(".sp").length || $(".spn").length) {
          var topHeight = $("#gb-template-top").height();
          $("#sp-content-outer, #spn-content-outer").css("margin-top",topHeight);
        }
        
        var sitenameContWidth = $("#gb-sitename-container").width();
        if($(window).width() >= 1024) {
    		$(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 20);
        }
        if($(window).width() < 1024 && $(window).width() >= 768) {
    		$(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 70);
        }
        if($(window).width() < 768 && $(window).width() >= 640) {
    		$(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 140);
        }
        
        $(".hp .cs-content-container .ui-widget.app.headlines .ui-article").each(function() {
        	var thisArticle = this;
            var thisThumbHeight = $(".ui-article-thumb img",this).height();
            $("div.clear",thisArticle).before("<div class='cs-headline-info-outer'><div class='cs-headline-info'></div></div>");
            $(".ui-article-description",thisArticle).prependTo($(this).find(".cs-headline-info"));
            $(".ui-article-title",thisArticle).prependTo($(this).find(".cs-headline-info"));
            
            //$(this).find(".cs-headline-info-outer").height(thisThumbHeight);
        });
        
        windowloadjsMediaQueries();
        
        $(".gb-school-list-header").click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			// IF THE SELECTED TAB ISNT ALREADY ACTIVE
			if(!$(this).hasClass("active")){
				// GET CLASS OF SELECTED TAB
				var selectedList = $(this).attr("class");
				selectedList = jQuery.trim(selectedList.replace("gb-school-list-header ", ""));
				
				//REMOVE CURRENT ACTIVE CLASSES
				$(".gb-school-list-header.active, .gb-school-list-section.active").removeClass("active");
				
				// SET NEW ACTIVE CLASSES
				$(this).addClass("active");
				$(".gb-school-list-section." + selectedList).addClass("active");
			}
		});
        $(".gb-school-list-header").keydown(function(e) {
        	if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if(!$(this).hasClass("active")){
                  // GET CLASS OF SELECTED TAB
                  var selectedList = $(this).attr("class");
                  selectedList = jQuery.trim(selectedList.replace("gb-school-list-header ", ""));

                  //REMOVE CURRENT ACTIVE CLASSES
                  $(".gb-school-list-header.active, .gb-school-list-section.active").removeClass("active");

                  // SET NEW ACTIVE CLASSES
                  $(this).addClass("active");
                  $(".gb-school-list-section." + selectedList).addClass("active");
				}
            }
        });
        
        $(window).resize(function() {
        	var newwindowHeight = $(window).height();
        	$(".hp #gb-template-top").height(newwindowHeight);
        });
        
        var setGalleryHeight = $("#gb-template-top").height();
        if($(".hp").length && $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container").height() < setGalleryHeight) {
          $("#hp-slideshow").addClass("no-height");
          $("#hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-container, #hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images, #hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images li, #hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-images ul.rs-gallery-images-list").css({
          	"height": setGalleryHeight
          });
          $("#hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-images ul.rs-gallery-images-list li img").css({
          	"margin-top": "0"
          });
        }
        
	});
    
    $(window).scroll(function() {
    	//if($(window).scrollTop() == $(document).height()- $(window).height()) {
            var stickyChannels = $(window).height() - $("#gb-channel-list-outer").height();
            stickyChannels = stickyChannels - 120;
            var getChannelPos = $("#gb-channel-list-outer").position();
            var scrolled = $(window).scrollTop();
            if($(".hp").length && $(window).width() > 1023) {
              if($(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").hasClass("clicked")) {
              	var schoollistHeight = $("#cs-schoollist-outer").height();
                schoollistHeight = schoollistHeight + 118 + 66;
                schoollistHeight = $(window).height() - schoollistHeight;
                if(scrolled > schoollistHeight) {
                	$("#cs-schoollist-outer").appendTo("#sticky-header-cont").css({
                      "position": "relative",
                      "top": "auto",
                      "bottom": "auto",
                      "left": "auto"
                    });
                	$("#gb-channel-list-outer").appendTo("#sticky-header-cont").css({
                      "position": "relative",
                      "top": "auto",
                      "bottom": "auto",
                      "left": "auto"
                    });
                    $("#gb-header-outer").css({
                          "background": "#FFF",
                          "box-shadow": "0 4px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.25)",
                          "z-index": "7010"
                    });
                    $(".sw-channel-dropdown-outer").addClass("position-below");
                } else {
                	$("#gb-channel-list-outer").appendTo("#gb-template-top").css({
                          "position": "absolute",
                          "top": "auto",
                          "bottom": "0",
                          "left": "0"
                        });
                        $("#gb-header-outer").css({
                              "background": "transparent none",
                              "box-shadow": "0 0 0",
                              "z-index": "100"
                        });
                        $(".sw-channel-dropdown-outer").removeClass("position-below");
                }
                var setHeight = $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li").height();
                    $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li").height(setHeight);

                    if(setHeight < $(window).height()) {
                        setHeight = $(window).height();
                        $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li img").height(setHeight);
                    }
              } else {
              		if(scrolled >= stickyChannels) {
                          $("#gb-channel-list-outer").appendTo("#sticky-header-cont").css({
                            "position": "relative",
                            "top": "auto",
                            "bottom": "auto",
                            "left": "auto"
                          });
                          $("#gb-header-outer").css({
                                "background": "#FFF",
                                "box-shadow": "0 4px 3px rgba(0,0,0,.25)",
                                "z-index": "7010"
                          });
                          $(".sw-channel-dropdown-outer").addClass("position-below");
                    } else {
                        $("#gb-channel-list-outer").appendTo("#gb-template-top").css({
                          "position": "absolute",
                          "top": "auto",
                          "bottom": "0",
                          "left": "0"
                        });
                        $("#gb-header-outer").css({
                              "background": "transparent none",
                              "box-shadow": "0 0 0",
                              "z-index": "100"
                        });
                        $(".sw-channel-dropdown-outer").removeClass("position-below");
                    }

                    var setHeight = $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li").height();
                    $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li").height(setHeight);

                    if(setHeight < $(window).height()) {
                        setHeight = $(window).height();
                        $("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li, #hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-container .rs-gallery-images .rs-gallery-images-list li img").height(setHeight);
                    }
              }
            }
        //}
    });
	
	$(function(){
		// SET IE CLASSES TO BODY
		if(isMSIE){ $("body").addClass("msie"); }
		if(isMSIE7){ $("body").addClass("msie7"); }
		if(isMSIE8){ $("body").addClass("msie8"); }
		if(isMSIE9){ $("body").addClass("msie9"); }
		if(isMSIE10){ $("body").addClass("msie10"); }
		if(isMSIE11){ $("body").addClass("msie11"); }
		$("body").addClass(navigator.platform + " " + browserName + " " + browserName + browserVersion);
	
		$(window).bind("resize", function(){ 
			jsMediaQueries(); 
			calendarListView();
            var sitenameContWidth = $("#gb-sitename-container").width();
            if($(window).width() >= 1024) {
                $(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 20);
            }
            if($(window).width() < 1024 && $(window).width() >= 768) {
                $(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 70);
            }
            if($(window).width() < 768 && $(window).width() >= 640) {
                $(".header-transparent-bg").css("left",sitenameContWidth + 140);
            }
            $(".hp #gb-template-top").height(windowHeight);
		});
        $("#cs-schoollist-outer").load("/cms/lib/TX01918059/Centricity/Template/20/schoollist/lubbock-school-menu.html", function(){});
		
        globalIcons();
        csRsMenu();
		jsMediaQueries();
		useChannelForSection();
        addFramesetTranslate();
		dynamicContent();
		mediaRotator();	
        socialMediaTabs();
        headlineMoreLinkCheck(); //Adam - 11.2.17 - 02969891
	});
    
    function headlineMoreLinkCheck(){
    	if($(".hp-content.one .headlines .more-link").length){
            $(".hp-content.one .headlines").addClass("has-more-link");
        }
    }

    
    function socialMediaTabs() {
    	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp").addClass("ui-clear").tabBlocks();
        
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button .tab-right").addClass("social-icon-tab");
        
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(0)").addClass("twitter-tab");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(1)").addClass("facebook-tab");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(2)").addClass("instagram-tab");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(3)").addClass("youtube-tab");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(4)").addClass("snapchat-tab");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(5)").addClass("vimeo-tab");
        
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(0) .tab-right").html("");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(1) .tab-right").html("");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(2) .tab-right").html("");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(3) .tab-right").html("");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(4) .tab-right").html("");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tabs-container .tab-button:eq(5) .tab-right").html("");
        
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(0)").addClass("twitter-feed");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(1)").addClass("facebook-feed");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(2)").addClass("instagram-feed");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(3)").addClass("youtube-feed");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(4)").addClass("snapchat-feed");
        $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel:eq(5)").addClass("vimeo-feed");
        
        if('true' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.twitter-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.twitter-feed").show();
        }
        if('true' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.facebook-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.facebook-feed").show();
        }
        if('false' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.instagram-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.instagram-feed").show();
        }
        if('false' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.youtube-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.youtube-feed").show();
        }
        if('false' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.snapchat-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.snapchat-feed").show();
        }
        if('false' == 'true') {
        	$("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-button.vimeo-tab, #sw-content-container6.ui-hp .tab-panel.vimeo-feed").show();
        }
    }
	
	function jsMediaQueries() {
		switch(csGetBreakPoint()) {
			case "desktop": 
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                  iconSlider();
                }  
			break;
			case "768":
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                  iconSlider();
                }
				appView();
			break;
			case "640":
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                  iconSlider();
                }
				appView();
			break;
			case "480":
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                  iconSlider();
                }
				appView();
			break;
			case "320":
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                  iconSlider();
                }
				appView();
			break;
		}
	}
    
    function windowloadjsMediaQueries() {
		switch(csGetBreakPoint()) {
			case "desktop": 
            	if($(".hp").length) {
                    importantHeadlines();
                }
			break;
			case "768":
                if(!$(".cs-content-container #slideshow-content-overlay-outer").length) {
                	$("#slideshow-content-overlay-outer").prependTo(".cs-content-container");
                }
			break;
			case "640":
            	
			break;
			case "480":
            	
			break;
			case "320":
            	
			break;
		}
	}
    
    function importantHeadlines() {
    	$("<div id='headlines-images-slideout-outer'><div class='headlines-images-slideout'></div></div>").prependTo("#slideshow-content-overlay");
    	$("#slideshow-content-overlay .ui-widget.app.headlines .ui-articles li").each(function() {
        	var getThis = this;
            if(!$(".ui-article-thumb",this).length) {
            	$(getThis).hide();
            }
            $(this).find(".ui-article-thumb").appendTo(".headlines-images-slideout");
        });
    	$("<button class='headline-images-toggle' aria-label='view headlines images' aria-expanded='false' aria-controls='headlines-images-slideout-outer'></button>").prependTo("#slideshow-content-overlay");	
    }

    function gbIconScroller() {
		var getWidth = $(window).width();
        var slideIconWidth = $("#hp-icon-slider-inner a").outerWidth();
        var numSliderIcons = 8;
        var sliderWidth = slideIconWidth * numSliderIcons;
		//DOC custom global icons scrolling
		if(numSliderIcons > 4 && getWidth >= 640) {
			$("#hp-icon-slider").css({
            	//"position": "absolute",
                //"display": "block",
                "width": sliderWidth
            });
            
            // ANIMATE THE ICON SLIDE   
            var timeout = setTimeout("runTimer()", 8000);
            
            $(".icon-slider-btn").click(function(e) {
            	//clearTimeout(timeout);
                e.preventDefault();
                var scrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider-inner a").outerWidth();
                var firstScrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider a").first().outerWidth(true);
                var lastScrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider a").last().outerWidth(true);
                var slidePos = parseInt($("#hp-icon-slider").css("margin-left")) * -1;
                var overflowDistance = parseInt($("#hp-icon-slider").css("width")) - $("#hp-icon-slider-inner").width();
                var lastScroll = overflowDistance - slidePos;
                var newPos = 0;

             
                if($(this).hasClass("next")) {
                    if(lastScroll < lastScrollDistance) {
                        newPos = 0;
                    } else {
                        newPos = slidePos + scrollDistance;
                    } 

                    $("#hp-icon-slider").animate({
                        marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
                    }, 800);
                    
                    var timeout = setTimeout("runTimer()",8000);
                    
                } else if($(this).hasClass("back")) {
                    if(slidePos < firstScrollDistance) {
                        newPos = lastScrollDistance;
                    } else {
                        newPos = slidePos - scrollDistance;
                    }

                    $("#hp-icon-slider").animate({
                        marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
                    }, 800);
                    
                    var timeout = setTimeout("runTimer()",8000);
                }
                
                
                
                $(".icon-slider-btn.back").keydown(function(e) {
                    if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if(lastScroll < lastScrollDistance) {
                            newPos = 0;
                        } else {
                            newPos = slidePos + scrollDistance;

                        } 

                        $("#hp-icon-slider").animate({
                            marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
                        }, 800);
                    }
                });
                
                $(".icon-slider-btn.back").focusout(function() {
                	$("#hp-icon-slider .global-icon").first().focus();
                });
                
                $(".icon-slider-btn.next").keydown(function(e) {
                	if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if(slidePos < firstScrollDistance) {
                            newPos = lastScrollDistance;
                        } else {
                            newPos = slidePos - scrollDistance;
                        }

                        $("#hp-icon-slider").animate({
                            marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
                        }, 800);
                    }
                });
            });
            
            
		} else if (numSliderIcons <= 4 && getWidth >= 640) {
        	$(".icon-slider-btn").hide();
        }
	}
    
    function runTimer() {
    	var scrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider-inner a").outerWidth();
        var firstScrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider a").first().outerWidth(true);
        var lastScrollDistance = $("#hp-icon-slider a").last().outerWidth(true);
        var slidePos = parseInt($("#hp-icon-slider").css("margin-left")) * -1;
        var overflowDistance = parseInt($("#hp-icon-slider").css("width")) - $("#hp-icon-slider-inner").width();
        var lastScroll = overflowDistance - slidePos;
        var newPos = 0;
        
        setTimeout(function() {
        	$('.icon-slider-btn.next').trigger('click');
        
            if(lastScroll < lastScrollDistance) {
                newPos = 0;
            } else {
                newPos = slidePos + scrollDistance;

            } 
            $("#hp-icon-slider").animate({
                marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
            }, 800);
        }, 8000);
        
        
        /*$("#hp-icon-slider").hover(function() {
            $("#hp-icon-slider").stop();
        }, function() {
            //var timeout = setTimeout("runTimer()", 1000);
        });*/
    }

    function csRsMenu() {
        var gradebookHeader = "GradeBook", popLinksHeader = "", popLinksMenu = "", elemHeader = "Elementary Schools", middleHeader = "Middle Schools", highHeader = "High Schools", otherHeader = "Other Schools";
        //GRADEBOOK RS MENU
        var gradebookMenu = "2, Parents, https://teams.lubbockisd.org/selfserve/EntryPointHomeAction.do?parent=true, _blank;2, Students, https://teams.lubbockisd.org/selfserve/EntryPointHomeAction.do?parent=false, _blank;2, Teachers, https://teams.lubbockisd.org/common/EntryPointSignOnAction.do, _blank";
    	
        //GLOBAL ICONS RS MENU
        var globalIcons = [
          ["Communication/12.png", "Eduphoria-Helpdesk", "/EduphoriaHelp ", "_blank"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["Student Program/4.png", "Meal Information", "/MealInfo  ", "_blank"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["/cms/lib/TX01918059/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/icons/review360-rev.png", "Review 360", "/Review360", "_blank"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["Site Utility/7.png", "Staff Directory", "/StaffDirect", "_blank"],
          ["Communication/18.png", "Staff Email", "/staffemail", "_self"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["/cms/lib/TX01918059/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/icons/Grey-TEAMS-logo.png", "Employee Svc. Center", "/ServiceCenter", "_blank"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["/cms/lib/TX01918059/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/icons/Grey-TEAMS-logo.png", "TEAMS", "/TEAMS1", "_blank"], // ARRAY ORDER - IMAGE, TEXT, LINK, TARGET
          ["Classroom/2.png", "Icon", "#", "_self"]
        ];
        var iconNum = ("7" == "8;7;6;5;4;3;2;1;0") ? 0 : "7";

        if(iconNum > 0) {
            popLinksHeader = "Popular Links";
        }

        for(var i = 0; i < iconNum; i++) {
            var linkCheck = (globalIcons[i][1] == "[SITECALENDARLINK]") ? "/Page/2" : globalIcons[i][2];
            popLinksMenu += '1,' + globalIcons[i][1] + ',' + linkCheck + ',' + globalIcons[i][3] + ';';
        }
        
    	// RESPONSIVE MENU
		$("body").csRsMenu({
			"breakPoint"			: 768, // SYSTEM BREAK POINTS - 768, 640, 480, 320
			"primaryColor"          : "#1A1A1A", // DEFAULT - #1A1A1A
		    "secondaryColor"        : "#0C0C0C", // DEFAULT - #0C0C0C
		    "accentColor"           : "#BABABA", // DEFAULT - #BABABA
			"menuButtonParent"		: "#gb-header-outer",
			"showMenuBtnText"		: "no",
			"menuBtnText"			: "MENU",
			"showSchools"			: "yes",
			"showTranslate"			: "yes",
			"translateId"			: "none",
			"showAccount"			: "yes",
			"extraMenuOptions"		: popLinksHeader + ";" + gradebookHeader, // EXTRA MENU HEADING NAMES SEPARATED BY A ;
			"extraMenuItems"		: popLinksMenu + gradebookMenu, // EXTRA MENU BUTTONS - STRUCTURE IS: MENU-OPTION-NUMBER, ITEM-NAME, ITEM-URL, ITEM-TARGET;
			"siteID"				: "4"
		});
        
        //var districtHomeLink = $(".sw-mystart-button.home > a").attr("href");
        //$("<li><a href='"+districtHomeLink+"'>District Home</a></li>").prependTo("#rs-menu ul.rs-menu-option-list");
    }
	
	function mediaRotator(windowHeight,channelBarHeight){
		if(!$("#sw-content-container10.region.ui-hp .rs-gallery-images").length){
			$("#sw-content-container10.ui-hp div.ui-widget.app.cs-rs-multimedia-rotator").csRsMultimediaRotator({
				"imageWidth" 					: 1500,
		        	"imageHeight" 				: 915,
		        	"appHeader" 				: "no",
		        	"titles" 					: "yes",
		        	"captions" 					: "yes",
		        	"galleryOverlay" 			: "yes",
		       		"linkedElement" 			: [""], // ["image", "title", "overlay", "all"]
		        	"playPause" 				: "no",
		        	"mainControls" 				: "yes",
		        	"contMoreLink" 				: "no",
		        	"contMoreLinkText" 			: "Learn More",
		        	"descMoreLink" 				: "yes",
		        	"descMoreLinkText" 			: "Learn More",
		        	"bullets" 					: "no",
		        	"bulletControls" 			: "no",
		        	"thumbnails" 				: "no",
		        	"thumbnailWidth" 			: 122,
		        	"thumbnailHeight" 			: 53,
		        	"thumbnailSlideDirection" 	: "horizontal", // horizontal or vertical
		        	"hoverPause" 				: "yes",
		        	"fullScreenRotator" 		: "yes", // image dimensions work well at 1500x915
		        	"fullScreenBreakpoints"   	: ["960", "768", "640", "480", "320"], // OPTIONS ARE ["960", "768", "640", "480", "320"]
		        	"fullScreenVideo" 			: "no",
		        	"transitionType" 			: "fade", // fade or slide
		        	"transitionSpeed" 			: 3,
		        	"transitionDelay" 			: 8,
					"autoRotate" 				: "yes",
		        	"onImageLoad" 				: function() { },
		        	"allImagesLoaded" 			: function() { },
		        	"onThumbnailLoad" 			: function() { },
		        	"allThumbnailsLoaded" 		: function() { },
		        	"onTransitionStart" 		: function() { },
		        	"onTransitionEnd" 			: function() { },
		        	"watchVidClick" 			: function() { },
		        	"closeVidClick" 			: function() { },
		        	"allLoaded" 				: function() {
                    	var setGalleryHeight = $("#gb-template-top").height();
                        $("#hp-slideshow").addClass("no-height");
                        $("#hp-slideshow.no-height .rs-gallery-container").css({
                          "height": setGalleryHeight+"px !important"
                        });
                    }
			});
		}
	}
	
	function appView(){
    	if($(".hp").length) {
          //DOC dont add app into accordion if it doesnt have a header
          $(".hp-content div.ui-widget.app").each(function() {
              if($(".ui-widget-header", this).hasClass("ui-helper-hidden") || jQuery.trim($(".ui-widget-header h1", this).text()) == "") {
                  $(this).addClass("no-header");
              }else{
                  if( $('.ui-widget-header h1 span.accordion-handle', this).length <= 0){
                      $('.ui-widget-header h1', this).append('<span class="accordion-handle hide960 show768 rotate-arrow"></span>');
                  }
              }
          });

          //DOC accordion header click
          $(".hp-content div.ui-widget-header").off('click').click(function(){
              var clickedApp = $(this).parent();

              if($(clickedApp).hasClass('active')){
                  $(clickedApp).removeClass('active');
                  $('.accordion-handle', clickedApp).removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
              }else{
                  $(".hp-content div.ui-widget.app.active .accordion-handle").removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
                  $(".hp-content div.ui-widget.app.active").removeClass("active");

                  $('.accordion-handle', clickedApp).removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
                  $(this).parent().addClass("active");
              }

              smoothScroll("#" + $(clickedApp).parent().attr("id"), 10);
          });
        } else if($(".sp").length) {
           $(".ui-widget.app.navigation.pagenavigation").addClass("active"); //added by Lyndsay - Case 00476403 - 2.2.17
          //DOC accordion header click
          $(".sp.column.one div.ui-widget-header").off('click').click(function(){
              var clickedApp = $(this).parent();

              if($(clickedApp).hasClass('active')){
                  $(clickedApp).removeClass('active');
                  $('.accordion-handle', clickedApp).removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
              }else{
                  $("#hp-content div.ui-widget.app.active .accordion-handle").removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
                  $("#hp-content div.ui-widget.app.active").removeClass("active");

                  $('.accordion-handle', clickedApp).removeClass('rotate-arrow').addClass('rotate-arrow');
                  $(this).parent().addClass("active");
              }

              smoothScroll("#" + $(clickedApp).parent().attr("id"), 10);
          });
        }
	}	
	
	function useChannelForSection(){
		//DOC use channel name for pagelistnavigation header if one is not present
		if(!$("div.sp.column.one .ui-widget-header h1").length > 0) {
			$("div.sp.column.one .ui-widget-header").append("<h1></h1>");
		}
    }
        
	function dynamicContent(){
		// ********** MYSTART ********** //
        //DOC move mystart buttons
        $(".sw-mystart-button.home").addClass('true').prependTo(".cs-mystart.top");
        $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a span").addClass("lubbock-icon-font").html("");
        $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a").attr("tabindex","-1");
        if($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey").length) {
        	$("#gb-search-btn").after($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey"));
        }
        $("#sw-search-button").attr("tabindex","-1");
        
        
            if($(".sw-mystart-button.register").length) {
                var registerBtn = $(".sw-mystart-button.register").html();
                $("<li>" + registerBtn + "</li>").prependTo("#user-options-dropdown ul");
                $(".sw-mystart-button.register").hide();
            }
        	if($(".sw-mystart-button.signin").length) {
                var signinBtn = $(".sw-mystart-button.signin").html();
                $("<li>" + signinBtn + "</li>").prependTo("#user-options-dropdown ul");
                $(".sw-mystart-button.signin").hide();
            }
        
        
		//UNBIND SYSTEM CLICK EVENT - MYSTART DROPDOWNS
		$(document).off("click", ".sw-mystart-dropdown");
		$(document).on("click", ".sw-mystart-dropdown", function(e) {
        	$(".sw-dropdown-arrow",this).addClass("rotate-arrow");
			$(".sw-dropdown", this).slideDown(300, "swing").attr('aria-hidden', 'true');;
			$(this).addClass("open");
		});
		$(".sw-mystart-dropdown").hover(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
		}, function() {
        	$(".sw-dropdown-arrow",this).removeClass("rotate-arrow");
			$(".sw-dropdown",this).slideUp(300, "swing");
			$(this).removeClass("open");
		});
        $(document).off("focus", ".sw-mystart-dropdown");
		$(document).on("focus", ".sw-mystart-dropdown", function(e) {
			$(".sw-dropdown", this).slideDown(300, "swing").attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
            $("#gb-mystart-inner").addClass("dropdown-active");
			$(this).addClass("open");
		});
        $(".sw-mystart-dropdown").focusout(function() {
        	$("#gb-mystart-inner").removeClass("dropdown-active");
			$(this).removeClass("open");
		});
        $(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate li a").keydown(function(e) {
			// CAPTURE KEY CODE
			switch(e.keyCode) {
				// CONSUME LEFT AND UP ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.left:
				case csKeyCodes.up:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($(this).parent().is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .selector").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$(this).parent().prev("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME RIGHT AND DOWN ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.right:
				case csKeyCodes.down:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($(this).parent().is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .sw-dropdown-list li:first-child > a").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$(this).parent().next("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME HOME KEY
				case csKeyCodes.home:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .sw-dropdown-list li:first-child > a").focus();
				break;
				
				// CONSUME END KEY
				case csKeyCodes.end:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .sw-dropdown-list li:last-child > a").focus();
				break;
                
                // CONSUME TAB KEY
				case csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").focus();
                    //CLOSE DROPDOWN
                    $(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .sw-dropdown").attr("aria-hidden","false").slideUp();
				break;
			
			}
		});
        
        $(document).on("click",".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist", function() {
            if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
              $(this).removeClass("clicked");
              $("#cs-schoollist-outer").attr("tabindex","-1").removeClass("open").slideUp();
            } else {
            	$(this).addClass("clicked");
            	$("#cs-schoollist-outer").attr("tabindex","0").addClass("open").slideDown();
            }
        });
        
        //SCHOOLLIST
        $(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").keydown(function(e) {
        	if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
                  $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Schools Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                  $("#cs-schoollist-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
                  $("#cs-schoollist-outer").attr("tabindex","-1");
                } else {
                    $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Schools Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
                    $("#cs-schoollist-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                    $("#cs-schoollist-outer .gb-school-list-header").first().focus();
                    $("#cs-schoollist-outer ul li a").attr("tabindex","0");
                    $("#cs-schoollist-outer li.last a").focusout(function() {
                        $(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").focus();
                    });
                    
                    if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.tab && e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.shift) {
                    	$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").focus();
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        $(".gb-school-list-column.elem li a").keydown(function(e) {
			// CAPTURE KEY CODE
			switch(e.keyCode) {
				// CONSUME LEFT AND UP ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.left:
				case csKeyCodes.up:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($(this).parent().is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$(".sw-mystart-dropdown.translate .selector").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$(this).parent().prev("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME RIGHT AND DOWN ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.right:
				case csKeyCodes.down:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($(this).parent().is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$(".gb-school-list-column.elem li:first-child > a").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$(this).parent().next("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME HOME KEY
				case csKeyCodes.home:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
					$(".gb-school-list-column.elem.elem li:first-child > a").focus();
				break;
				
				// CONSUME END KEY
				case csKeyCodes.end:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".gb-school-list-column.elem li:last-child > a").focus();
				break;
                
                // CONSUME TAB KEY
				case csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").focus();
				break;
                
                case csKeyCodes.shift+csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-schoollist").focus();
				break;
			
			}
		});
        
        
        
        //UNBIND SYSTEM CLICK EVENT - MY ACCOUNT
        $(document).off("click", "#sw-mystart-account");
		$(document).on("click", "#sw-mystart-account", function(e) {
        	$(".sw-myaccount-chevron",this).addClass("rotate-arrow");
			$("#sw-myaccount-list", this).slideDown(300, "swing");
			$(this).addClass("open");
		});
		$("#sw-myaccount-list").hover(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
		}, function() {
        	$(".sw-myaccount-chevron",this).removeClass("rotate-arrow");
			$("#sw-myaccount-list",this).slideUp(300, "swing");
			$(this).removeClass("open");
		});
        
        $("#user-options-dropdown li").last().addClass("last");
        
        $(document).on("click",".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options", function() {
            if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
              $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close User Options Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
              $("#user-options-dropdown-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
              if($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey").length) {
              	  $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a").attr("tabindex","-1");
                  $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button").css({
                  	"right": "-49px"
                  });
                  $("#gb-search-btn").css({
                      "right": "0"
                  });
                }
            } else {
            	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open User Options Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
            	$("#user-options-dropdown-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                if($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey").length) {
                  $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a").attr("tabindex","0");
                  $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button").css({
                  	"right": "0"
                  });
                  $("#gb-search-btn").css({
                      "right": "49px"
                  });
                }
            }
        });
        
        $(".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options").keydown(function(e) {
        	if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
                  $(this).removeClass("clicked");
                  $("#user-options-dropdown-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
                  $("#user-options-dropdown ul li a").attr("tabindex","-1");
                  if($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey").length) {
                  	$("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a").attr("tabindex","-1");
                    $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button").css({
                      "right": "-49px"
                    });
                    $("#gb-search-btn").css({
                        "right": "0"
                    });
                  }
                } else {
                    $(this).addClass("clicked");
                    $("#user-options-dropdown-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                    $("#user-options-dropdown ul li:eq(0) a").focus();
                    $("#user-options-dropdown ul li a").attr("tabindex","0");
                    $("#user-options-dropdown li.last a").focusout(function() {
                        $(".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options").focus();
                    });
                    if($("#sw-mystart-mypasskey").length) {
                      $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button > a").attr("tabindex","0");
                      $("#sw-mystart-mypasskey.sw-mystart-button").css({
                        "right": "0"
                      });
                      $("#gb-search-btn").css({
                          "right": "49px"
                      });
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        
        $(".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options").keydown(function(e) {
			// CAPTURE KEY CODE
			switch(e.keyCode) {
				// CONSUME LEFT AND UP ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.left:
                e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$("#user-options-dropdown li:last-child a").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().prev("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
                 break;
				case csKeyCodes.up:
                	// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$("#user-options-dropdown li:last-child a").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().prev("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME RIGHT AND DOWN ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.right:
                e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a:first-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().next("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				case csKeyCodes.down:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a:first-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$("#user-options-dropdown li a").parent().next("li").find("> a").focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME HOME KEY
				case csKeyCodes.home:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
					$("#user-options-dropdown li a:first-child").focus();
				break;
				
				// CONSUME END KEY
				case csKeyCodes.end:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$("#user-options-dropdown li a:last-child").focus();
				break;
                
                // CONSUME TAB KEY
				case csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options").focus();
				break;
                
                case csKeyCodes.shift+csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.cs-user-options").focus();
				break;
			
			}
		});
        
        $(document).off("focus", "#sw-mystart-account");
		$(document).on("focus", "#sw-mystart-account", function(e) {
			$("#sw-myaccount-list", this).slideDown(300, "swing").attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
			$(this).addClass("open");
		});
        $("#sw-mystart-account").focusout(function() {
			$(this).removeClass("open");
		});
        
        //POPULAR LINKS BTN CLICK
        $(document).off("click", ".sw-mystart-button.popular-links");
        $(document).on("click", ".sw-mystart-button.popular-links", function() {
        	if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
              $(this).removeClass("clicked");
              $("#gb-icons-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
            } else {
            	$(this).addClass("clicked");
            	$("#gb-icons-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
            }
        });
        $(".sw-mystart-button.popular-links").keydown(function(e) {
          if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
              e.preventDefault();
              if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
                $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Popular Links Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                $("#gb-icons-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
              } else {
                  $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Popular Links Menu",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
                  $("#gb-icons-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                  $("#gb-global-icons .global-icon").first().focus();
                  $("#gb-global-icons .global-icon").last().focusout(function() {
                  	$(".sw-mystart-button.popular-links").focus();
                  });
              }
          }
         });
         
         $("#gb-global-icons a").keydown(function(e) {
			// CAPTURE KEY CODE
			switch(e.keyCode) {
				// CONSUME LEFT AND UP ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.left:
                e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($(this).is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$("gb-global-icons a:last-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$(this).prev().focus();
					}
                 break;
				case csKeyCodes.up:
                	// IS FIRST ITEM
					if($(this).is(":first-child")) {
						// FOCUS DROPDOWN BUTTON
						$("gb-global-icons a:last-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS PREVIOUS ITEM
						$(this).prev().focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME RIGHT AND DOWN ARROWS
				case csKeyCodes.right:
                e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($(this).is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$("gb-global-icons a:first-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$(this).next().focus();
					}
				break;
				case csKeyCodes.down:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// IS LAST ITEM
					if($(this).is(":last-child")) {
						// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
						$("gb-global-icons a:first-child").focus();
					} else {
						// FOCUS NEXT ITEM
						
						$(this).next().focus();
					}
				break;
				
				// CONSUME HOME KEY
				case csKeyCodes.home:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS FIRST ITEM
					$("gb-global-icons a:first-child").focus();
				break;
				
				// CONSUME END KEY
				case csKeyCodes.end:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$("gb-global-icons a:last-child").focus();
				break;
                
                // CONSUME TAB KEY
				case csKeyCodes.tab:
					e.preventDefault();
					
					// FOCUS LAST ITEM
					$(".sw-mystart-button.popular-links").focus();
				break;
			
			}
		});
         
        $(document).off("click", ".headline-images-toggle");
        $(document).on("click", ".headline-images-toggle", function() {
        	if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
              $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
              $("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
            } else {
            	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
            	$("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                $(".headlines-images-slideout > a").last().focusout(function() {
                	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                    $("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
                    $("#slideshow-content-overlay .gb-scroll-down-btn").focus();
                });
            }
        });
        $(".headline-images-toggle").keydown(function(e) {
          if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
              e.preventDefault();
              if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
              		$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
              		$("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
            } else {
            	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
            	$("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").addClass("open").slideDown();
                $(".headlines-images-slideout > a").last().focusout(function() {
                	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Headline Images",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                    $("#headlines-images-slideout-outer").removeClass("open").slideUp();
                    $("#slideshow-content-overlay .gb-scroll-down-btn").focus();
                });
            }
          }
         });

        	if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
            	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Search Input",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                    $("#sw-search-input").attr("tabindex","-1");
                $("#gb-search-cont").removeClass("open");
                $("#gb-search-cont").css({
                    "right": "-676px"
                });
            } else {
            	$(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Search Input",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
                 $("#sw-search-input").attr("tabindex","0");
                $("#gb-search-cont").addClass("open");
                $("#gb-search-cont").css({
                    "right": "49px"
                });
            }
        });
        $("#gb-search-btn").keydown(function(e) {
          if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
              e.preventDefault();
              if($(this).hasClass("clicked")) {
                  $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Open Search Input",
                        "aria-expanded": "false"
                    }).removeClass("clicked");
                    $("#sw-search-input").attr("tabindex","-1");
                  $("#gb-search-cont").removeClass("open");
                  $("#gb-search-cont").css({
                      "right": "-676px"
                  });
                  $("#gb-search-cont").attr("tabindex","-1");
                  //$("#gb-search-btn").focus();
              } else {
                  $(this).attr({
                    	"aria-label": "Close Search Input",
                        "aria-expanded": "true"
                    }).addClass("clicked");
                 $("#sw-search-input").attr("tabindex","0");
                  $("#gb-search-cont").addClass("open");
                  $("#gb-search-cont").css({
                      "right": "49px"
                  });
                  $("#gb-search-cont").attr("tabindex","0");

        	e.preventDefault();
			$("html, body").animate({
				scrollTop: $(".cs-content-container").offset().top - 184
			}, 800, function(){
				$("html, body").stop(true, false);
			});
		});
        
        $('.gb-scroll-down-btn').on('keydown', function(e) { 
        // Trigger the click event from the keyboard 
          var code = e.which; 
          // 13 = Return, 32 = Space 
          if ((code === 13) || (code === 32)) { 
            $("html, body").animate({
				scrollTop: $(".cs-content-container").offset().top - 184
			}, 800, function(){
				$("html, body").stop(true, false);
			});
            $(".hp.column.one a").focus();
			return false;
          }

		$(".sw-channel-item").unbind('hover');
		$(".sw-channel-item").hover(function(){
			var subList = $(this).children('.sw-channel-dropdown-outer');
            $(subList).stop(true);
			if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
				subList.slideDown(300, "swing");
			}
			$(this).addClass("hover");
		}, function(){
			$(".sw-channel-dropdown-outer").slideUp(300, "swing");
			$(this).removeClass("hover");
		});

            });

            .not($("div.ui-widget.app.gallery.json .ui-widget-detail img"))
            .each(function() {
                if ($(this).attr('width') !== undefined && $(this).attr('height') !== undefined) { // IMAGE HAS INLINE DIMENSIONS
                    $(this).css({"display": "inline-block", "width": "100%", "max-width": $(this).attr("width") + "px", "height": "auto", "max-height": $(this).attr("height") + "px"});

        	e.preventDefault();

            });
            
        });
        $(".gb-scroll-to-top").keydown(function(e) {
        	if(e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.enter || e.keyCode == csKeyCodes.space) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow", function() {
                    $("#gb-logo a").focus();
                });
            }
        });
	}
	
	function eventsByDay(container) {
		var countLi = 0;
        var csMonth = "";
		$(".ui-article", container).each(function(){
			if (!$(".sw-calendar-block-date", this).length){
				var moveArticle = $(this).html();
				$(this).parent().prev().children().children().next().append(moveArticle);
				$(this).parent().remove();
			} else {
				$(".sw-calendar-block-date", this).wrapInner('<span class="joel-date"></span>');
				$(".joel-month", this).parents(".sw-calendar-block-date").prepend($(".joel-month", this));
			}
            
            //Add 'ALL DAY' Text to full day events
            $('.ui-article-description', this).each(function(){ 
                if( $('.sw-calendar-block-time', this).length < 1 ){ //if it doesnt exist add it
                    $(this).prepend('<span class="sw-calendar-block-time">ALL DAY</span>');
                }
            });
		});
        
        //Add 0 before single digit dates
        $(".upcomingevents .ui-article").each(function() {
        	// ADD ZERO TO DAY IF LESS THAN 10
            $(".joel-date", this).text(((parseInt($(".joel-date", this).text()) < 10) ? "0" : "") + $(".joel-date", this).text());
        });
        
        //Move event time below event title
        $('.ui-widget.app.upcomingevents .ui-widget-detail .ui-articles .ui-article-description').each(function(){
			$(".sw-calendar-block-time", this).before($(".sw-calendar-block-title",this));
		});
	}
	
	function searchText() {
		//DOC custom mystart search placeholder
	    //SEARCH TEXT
	    $("div#sw-mystart-search input#sw-search-input").removeAttr("placeholder");
		$("div#sw-mystart-search input#sw-search-input").attr("value", "I'm looking for...");
		$("div#sw-mystart-search input#sw-search-input").focus(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "I'm looking for...") {
				$(this).val("");
			}
		});
		$("div#sw-mystart-search input#sw-search-input").blur(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "") {
				$(this).val("I'm looking for...");
			}
		});
	}
	
	function calendarListView() {
		// AUTO CLICK FUNCTION FOR SCHOOLWIRES CALENDAR LIST VIEW FOR SMALL MOBILE DEVICES
		if(!$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview.loaded").length){
			$("a.ui-btn-toggle.list").click();
			$("a.ui-btn-toggle.month").click();
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").addClass("loaded");
		}
		
		switch(csGetBreakPoint()) {
			case "desktop": case "768": case "640":
				$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendar").removeClass("ui-helper-hidden");
				$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").addClass("ui-helper-hidden");
			break;
			case "480": case "320":
				$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendar").addClass("ui-helper-hidden");
				$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").removeClass("ui-helper-hidden");
				$(".ui-btn-toggle.month").removeClass("active");
				$(".ui-btn-toggle.list").addClass("active");
			break;
		}
	}
    
    function csGetBreakPoint() {
		return window.getComputedStyle(document.querySelector("body"), ":before").getPropertyValue("content").replace(/"|'/g, "");/*"*/
	}
	
	function hexToRgb(h){
	        var r = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(0,2),16);
	        var g = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(2,4),16);
	        var b = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(4,6),16);
	        return r+', '+g+', '+b;
	};
	 
	function cutHex(h) {
	        return (h.charAt(0)=="#") ? h.substring(1,7):h;
	};
	
	//usage
	//console.log(hexToRgb("#FFFFFF"));
	//usage with RGBA
	//console.log("rgba("+hexToRgb('#FFFFFF')+",0.5)");
